TI Experimental studies using a low-energy RI beam separator at CNS
SO NUCLEAR PHYSICS A
LA English

ID LIGHT-NUCLEI; C-12
AB Radioactive-ion (RI) beams of C-10, O-14, N-12 and C-11 with energies below 10 A MeV were produced by using a low-energy in-flight RI beam separator newly constructed by CNS, University of Tokyo. Using the N-12 and C-11 beams, some resonance states were identified in the proton elastic scattering N-12+p and C-11+p, respectively.

TI Study of resonance states in N-12 using a radioactive ion beam of C-11
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE resonance states; elastic scattering; radioactive ion beam; nuclear
   astrophysics
ID SCATTERING; NUCLEI
AB Resonance states in N-12 were studied by using the resonance elastic scattering of C-11 + p with a low-energy radioactive ion beam of C-11 at 3.5 MeV/nucleon and a thick (CH2)(n) target. The I I C beam was separated by a newly installed CNS radioactive ion beam separator (CRIB). The energy spectrum of recoil protons was measured at laboratory scattering angles around theta(LAB) = 0degrees to identify resonance states in 12N. The spin-parity values of J(pi) = 3(-) and (2)+ have been determined for the levels at the excitation energies of E-x =(.)3.1 and 3.6 MeV in N-12, respectively, suggesting a small contribution of the 3.1-MeV level to the C-11(p, gamma)N-12 stellar reaction. (C) 2003 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Net neutron-rich isotopes, Ne-34, Na-37 and Si-43, produced by
   fragmentation of a 64 A MeV Ca-48 beam
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID SHELL-MODEL; DRIP-LINE; PARTICLE STABILITY; NUCLEI; REGION; DEFORMATION;
   COLLECTIVITY; CLOSURE; SEARCH; MG-34
AB An experiment to the search for very neutron-rich nuclei has been performed at RIKEN, using projectile fragmentation of an intense 64 A MeV Ca-48 beam and the fragment separator RIPS. Three new neutron-rich isotopes, Ne-34, Na-37 and Si-43 were observed unambiguously for the first time, and convincing evidence for the particle instability of three others, Ne-33, Na-36 and Mg-39 was obtained. The experimental findings are discussed in comparison with recent theoretical predictions. (C) 2002 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Gamma-ray spectroscopy of Mg-34 via RI beam fragmentation
SO NUCLEAR PHYSICS A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 5th International Conference on Radioactive Nuclear Beams
CY MAR 27-APR 01, 2000
CL DIVONNE, FRANCE
SP CERN, ISOLDE
ID MASS MEASUREMENTS; DEFORMATION; ISOTOPES; COLLECTIVITY; NUCLEI
AB A novel technique with a radioactive isotope beam has been employed for in-beam gamma-ray spectroscopy of a very neutron-rich isotope Mg-34. The excited Mg-34 were produced by the projectile fragmentation reaction induced by a radioactive Si-36 beam at 50 MeV/nucleon on a 385 mg/cm(2) Be-9 target. Deexcitation gamma rays were detected in coincidence with the Mg-34 fragments. The measured excitation energy, 660 +/- 10 keV, implies a large deformation of Mg-34. (C) 2002 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Inelastic scattering on Be-12 and disappearance of the N=8 magic number
SO EUROPEAN PHYSICAL JOURNAL A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT International Symposium on Perspectives in Physics with Radioactive
   Isotope Beams 2000 (RIB00)
CY NOV 13-16, 2000
CL HAYAMA, JAPAN
SP RIKEN, RARF, Univ Tokyo, Ctr Nucl Study
ID COULOMB-EXCITATION; BETA-DECAY; DEFORMATION; SPECTROSCOPY; DESCENDANTS;
   TRANSITIONS; NUCLEI
AB Experimental studies on in-beam gamma-ray spectroscopy using a Be-12 radioactive beam are presented. Inelastic scattering of the neutron-rich Be-12 nucleus on Pb-208, C-12, and (CH2)(n) targets has been studied by measuring de-excitation gamma-rays in coincidence with scattered particles, The level schemes and transition probabilities are determined for low-lying excited states in Be-12. The present paper presents a brief review of the spectroscopic results, which may be associated with the N = 8 shell quenching near the drip line.

TI New low-energy RIB separator CRIB for nuclear astrophysics
SO EUROPEAN PHYSICAL JOURNAL A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT International Symposium on Perspectives in Physics with Radioactive
   Isotope Beams 2000 (RIB00)
CY NOV 13-16, 2000
CL HAYAMA, JAPAN
SP RIKEN, RARF, Univ Tokyo, Ctr Nucl Study
AB An in-flight RIB separator at low energies, which is the first extensive separator at low energies, called CRIB, is just under construction at CNS. This consists of a double-achromatic magnetic separator, a window-less gas target, and a Wien filter. Some characteristics of the CRIB are described. Possible experimental plans are also discussed in our nuclear astrophysics project for the study of the explosive hydrogen burning process, especially on the onset mechanism.

TI Coulomb dissociation of halo nuclei
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS SUPPLEMENT
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 10th Yukawa International Seminar on Physics of Unstable Nuclei
CY NOV 05-10, 2001
CL KYOTO, JAPAN
SP Univ Calif Santa Barbara, Inst Theoret Phys, Yukawa Mem Fdn, Commemorat Assoc Japan World Exposit 1970, Minist Educ, Culture, Sports, Sci & Technol Japan, Kyoto Univ Fdn, Inoue Fdn Sci, Kajima Fdn, Matsushita Elect Ind Co, Sanyo Elect Co, Omron corp, Asahi Breweries
HO KYOTO UNIV, YUKAWA INST THEORET PHYS
ID BREAKUP; BE-11
AB Coulomb dissociation of loosely bound nuclei Be-11 and C-15 have been studied in a kinematically complete measurement. For Be-11, the n-Be-10 relative energy spectrum has been analyzed as a function of the impact parameter, b. The obtained spectrum with b greater than or equal to 30 fm agrees very well with the first order perturbation theory assuming a pure Coulomb process. It suggests that a selection of the impact parameter is effective to exclude the higher order effect and the nuclear breakup contribution from the measured dissociation cross section. The spectroscopic factor for Be-10(0(+)) circle times 1s(1/2) in the ground state is then extracted to be 0.69(3). The result of C-15 has been applied to determine the C-14(n,gamma)C-15 cross section, which is relevant to the stellar nuclear synthesis such as the CNO cycle in low mass AGB stars. The obtained neutron capture cross section is consistent with that of the P-wave direct capture process.
C1 RIKEN, Wako, Saitama 3510198, Japan.
   Tokyo Inst Technol, Tokyo 1528551, Japan.
   Tohoku Univ, Dept Phys, Sendai, Miyagi 9808578, Japan.

TI Coulomb excitation of Si-24
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS SUPPLEMENT
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 10th Yukawa International Seminar on Physics of Unstable Nuclei
CY NOV 05-10, 2001
CL KYOTO, JAPAN
SP Univ Calif Santa Barbara, Inst Theoret Phys, Yukawa Mem Fdn, Commemorat Assoc Japan World Exposit 1970, Minist Educ, Culture, Sports, Sci & Technol Japan, Kyoto Univ Fdn, Inoue Fdn Sci, Kajima Fdn, Matsushita Elect Ind Co, Sanyo Elect Co, Omron corp, Asahi Breweries
HO KYOTO UNIV, YUKAWA INST THEORET PHYS
AB We have measured Coulomb excitation of Si-24 to its first excited state to obtain the E2 transition probability. This is the first measurement of B(E2) for a T-Z = -2 nucleus, which enables us to compare their transition probabilities between the mirror pair of T = 2, namely Si-24 and Ne-24.

TI Inelastic scattering of Be-12 with He-4
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS SUPPLEMENT
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 10th Yukawa International Seminar on Physics of Unstable Nuclei
CY NOV 05-10, 2001
CL KYOTO, JAPAN
SP Univ Calif Santa Barbara, Inst Theoret Phys, Yukawa Mem Fdn, Commemorat Assoc Japan World Exposit 1970, Minist Educ, Culture, Sports, Sci & Technol Japan, Kyoto Univ Fdn, Inoue Fdn Sci, Kajima Fdn, Matsushita Elect Ind Co, Sanyo Elect Co, Omron corp, Asahi Breweries
HO KYOTO UNIV, YUKAWA INST THEORET PHYS
AB Inelastic scattering of the neutron-rich nucleus Be-12 on a liquid-He target has been studied by measuring de-excitation gamma rays in coincidence with scattered Be-12. In the angular distribution, a difference between the 2(1)(+) and the 1(-) state in Be-12 was cleary seen.

TI Molecular states in neutron-rich beryllium isotopes
SO PROGRESS OF THEORETICAL PHYSICS SUPPLEMENT
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 10th Yukawa International Seminar on Physics of Unstable Nuclei
CY NOV 05-10, 2001
CL KYOTO, JAPAN
SP Univ Calif Santa Barbara, Inst Theoret Phys, Yukawa Mem Fdn, Commemorat Assoc Japan World Exposit 1970, Minist Educ, Culture, Sports, Sci & Technol Japan, Kyoto Univ Fdn, Inoue Fdn Sci, Kajima Fdn, Matsushita Elect Ind Co, Sanyo Elect Co, Omron corp, Asahi Breweries
HO KYOTO UNIV, YUKAWA INST THEORET PHYS
ID BE-12
AB Excited states in Be-12 and Be-14 were studied by using an exotic beam of Be-14 at 75 A MeV. A new excited state in Be-12 was observed at 11.8 MeV. The angular-correlation analysis showed that the spin for the new level is tentatively assigned to be 0. According to the energy-spin systematics, the observed state may be a member of the rotational band of the He-6-He-6 cluster structure. Three excited states in Be-14 were also found at 10.8 MeV, 11.6 MeV, and 15.5 MeV.

TI Large collectivity of Mg-34
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID NEUTRON-RICH NUCLEI; RELATIVISTIC MEAN-FIELD; N = 20;
   COULOMB-EXCITATION; SHELL CLOSURE; QUADRUPOLE COLLECTIVITY; INTERMEDIATE
   ENERGIES; SHAPE COEXISTENCE; MASS MEASUREMENTS; GIANT-RESONANCES
AB The highly neutron-rich nucleus Mg-34 has been studied via Coulomb excitation using a radioactive 34Mg beam at 44.9 MeV/nucleon with a Pb target. The B(E2; O-g.s.(+) --> 2(1)(+)) value for the previously proposed 2(1)(+) state in Mg-34 was determined for the first time to be 631(126) e(2) fm(4). This value corresponds to the quadrupole deformation parameter beta (2) of 0.58(6), implying an anomalously large deformation of Mg-34. (C) 2001 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Isobaric analog state of Be-14
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE isobaric analog state; charge-exchange reactions; radioactive beam
   experiment; Coulomb displacement energy; halo structure
ID N=8 SHELL CLOSURE; NUCLEAR RADII; LI-11; HALO
AB The Isobaric Analog State (IAS) of the neutron-dripline nucleus Be-14 has been found for the first time in a charge-exchange reaction Be-14(p, n)B-14* in inverse kinematics at E(Be-14) = 74 A MeV. The excitation energy and width of the observed IAS were measured to be 17.06 +/- 0.03 MeV and 0.11 +/- 0.05 MeV (FWHM), respectively. The Coulomb displacement energy and the measured width of the IAS are discussed in connection with a possible neutron-halo structure of the Be-14 nucleus. (C) 2001 Elsevier Science B.V. TI Deformation of Mg-34 studied via in-beam gamma-ray spectroscopy using
   radioactive-ion projectile fragmentation
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID DIRECT MASS MEASUREMENTS; RELATIVISTIC MEAN-FIELD; NEUTRON-RICH
   ISOTOPES; N = 20; COULOMB-EXCITATION; SHELL-MODEL; BETA-DECAY; NUCLEI;
   REGION; COLLECTIVITY
AB The location of low-lying states in the very neutron-rich isotope Mg-34 has been determined for the first time. In-beam gamma -ray spectroscopy was performed using a two-step fragmentation reaction. Two strong gamma -lines were observed at 660(10) keV and 1460(20) keV, which are tentatively attributed to the 2(1)(+) --> 0(g.s)(+) and 4(1)(+) --> 2(1)(+) transitions in Mg-34, respectively. These tentative assignments lead to a very low energy for the 2(1)(+) state and a large E (4(1)(+))/E(2(1)(+)) ratio of about 3.2, in agreement with the expectations for a well deformed isotope. (C) 2001 Published by Elsevier Science B.V.

TI Low-lying intruder 1(-) state in Be-12 and the melting of the N=8 shell
   closure
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID COULOMB DISSOCIATION; LI-11; EXCITATION; NUCLEUS; SPECTROSCOPY;
   TRANSITIONS
AB Inelastic scattering of the neutron-rich nucleus Be-12 on lead and carbon targets has been studied by measuring de-excitation gamma rays in coincidence with scattered Be-12. The strong gamma -ray transition from the state at E-x = 2.68(3) MeV following El Coulomb excitation was observed for the lead target, leading to an assignment of J(pi) = 1(-) for the excited state. The low excitation energy of this intruder 1(-) state and the deduced large B(El; O-g.s.(+) --> 1(-)) value of 0.051(13)e(2) fm(2) provide a consistent picture of the N = 8 shell melting in Be-12. (C) 2000 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Quadrupole deformation of Be-12 studied by proton inelastic scattering
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID NEUTRON-RICH NUCLEI; BETA-DECAY; RADIOACTIVE BEAM; ENERGY-LEVELS;
   LIGHT-NUCLEI; MODEL; TRANSITION; ISOTOPES; SPECTROSCOPY; DESCENDANTS
AB Inelastic proton scattering exciting the 2(1)(+) states in the neutron-rich beryllium isotopes Be-10,Be-12 has been studied in inverse kinematics. From a coupled-channel analysis, the deformation lengths for the 2(1)(+) states in Be-10 and Be-12 were determined to be 1.80 +/- 0.25 fm and 2.00 +/- 0.23 fm respectively, indicating that a tendency towards strong quadrupole deformation is preserved for these nuclei and that the singly-closed shell structure does not prevail in Be-12. A quantitative analysis based on shell model calculations supports this picture. (C) 2000 Elsevier Science B.V. All rights reserved.

TI Coulomb dissociation of C-19 and its halo structure
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW LETTERS
LA English
DT Article
ID ONE-NEUTRON HALO; ATOMIC MASS EVALUATION; LI-11; BE-11
AB The extremely neutron-rich nucleus C-19 has been studied by Coulomb dissociation into C-18 + n at 67 A MeV. A large E1 strength of 0.71 +/- 0.07 e(2) fm(2) has been observed at low excitation energies. An analysis of the angular distribution of C-18 + n Center Of mass has led to a determination of the neutron separation energy of C-19 to be 530 +/- 130 keV. The El strength distribution can be well reproduced for a C-19 ground state structure with a dominant s-wave valence neutron, providing a consistent picture of the neutron halo structure of C-19.

TI Further measurement of the Be-7(p,gamma)B-8 cross section at low
   energies with the coulomb dissociation of B-8
SO EUROPEAN PHYSICAL JOURNAL A
LA English
DT Article
ID BE-7(P
AB We have measured the dissociation of B-8 in the Coulomb field of Pb-208 at E-in=51.9 MeV/nucleon and extracted the cross section of the Be-7(p,gamma)B-8 reaction at 0.4 less than or equal to E-rel less than or equal to 3 MeV, which is of importance for the B-8 solar-neutrino production rate. The extracted astrophysical S-17 factors are consistent with our earlier Coulomb dissociation measurement, and agree with the values deduced from the direct capture measurements by Filippone et al., Vaughn et al. and Hammache et al. The S factor at zero energy wad; extracted to be 18.9+/-1.8 eV-b with the help of theoretical energy-dependence.

TI Isobaric analog state of Li-11
SO NUCLEAR PHYSICS A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 6th International Conference on Nucleus-Nucleus Collisions
CY JUN 02-06, 1997
CL GATLINBURG, TENNESSEE
SP US DOE, US Natl Sci Fdn, Oak Ridge Natl Lab, Michigan State Univ, Natl Superconducting Cyclotron Lab
ID BETA-DECAY; INTERMEDIATE ENERGIES; COULOMB DISSOCIATION; HALO STRUCTURE;
   LIGHT-NUCLEI; SCATTERING; NEUTRONS; BE-11
AB The isobaric analog state (IAS) of the Li-11 nucleus has been investigated using the (p,n) reaction in inverse kinematics at E(Li-11) = 64 A MeV. The IAS has been found in the decay energy spectrum of Be-11* --> Li-9+p+n at the corresponding excitation energy of 21.16+/-0.02 MeV with a width of 0.49+/-0.07 MeV (FWHM). The Coulomb displacement energy, decay width, decay mode and their relation to the halo structure are discussed.

TI beta decay of the neutron-rich isotope Be-14
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW C
LA English
DT Article
ID ENERGY-LEVELS
AB The neutron spectroscopy of the beta-delayed neutron decay of Be-14 has been investigated. A strong neutron group, which accounts for much of the P-decay yield and could explain the discrepancy in total neutron branching ratio found in a previous experiment, Was observed. We found that the total width of the final state for this transition is 60+/-5+/-6 keV, and the measured half-life of the Be-14 beta decay was 4.29+/-0.18 ms. The limits on the branching ratio and logft value determined for this group are compared with the earlier work and the results of a shell-model calculation.

TI Isobaric analog state of Li-11
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE halo nucleus; isobaric analog state; Coulomb displacement energy; charge
   exchange reactions; radioactive beam experiment
ID INTERMEDIATE ENERGIES; COULOMB DISSOCIATION; BETA-DECAY; SCATTERING
AB The isobaric analog state (IAS) of the halo nucleus Li-11 has been investigated using the charge exchange reaction Li-11(p,n)Be-11* in inverse kinematics at E(Li-11) = 64A MeV. The IAS was observed in Be-11, for the first time, at an excitation energy of 21.16 +/- 0.02 MeV with a width of 0.49 +/- 0.07 MeV (FWHM). The unit cross section, distortion factor and effective N-N interaction associated with the Fermi transition are extracted. Coulomb displacement energy, decay width, reaction variables and their relation to the halo structure are discussed. (C) 1997 Elsevier Science B.V.

TI Charge exchange reaction of the neutron-halo nucleus Li-11
SO NUCLEAR PHYSICS A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 4th International Conference on Radioactive Nuclear Beams
CY JUN 03-07, 1996
CL OMIYA, JAPAN
SP Inst Phys & Chem Res, Inst Nucl Study, Univ Tokyo, Int Union Pure & Appl Phys
ID BETA-DECAY; STATES
AB Charge exchange reactions of the Li-11 nucleus have been measured by means of the inverse kinematics on proton and deuteron targets at 63 A MeV. The isobaric analog state of the Li-11 nucleus has been found at E-r(Be-11) = 21.14 +/- 0.03 MeV with the width Gamma = 0.25 (+0.2)(-0.1) MeV. Neutron halo effects and the configuration of halo nucleons are discussed.

TI Coulomb excitation of Be-11
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE intermediate-energy Coulomb excitation; radioactive beam
ID RADIOACTIVE BEAM; ELECTROMAGNETIC-EXCITATION; BREAK-UP; DISSOCIATION;
   LI-11; COLLISIONS
AB The Coulomb excitation of a halo nucleus Be-11 to its first bound excited state (E1: 1/2(+)-->1/2(-)) has been studied using a 64 MeV/u Be-11 radioactive beam incident on a Pb-208 target. The electric dipole strength deduced by a first-order perturbation analysis is in good agreement with the result of previous life-time measurements of the Be-11 1/2(-) state.

TI Experimental determination of the E2 component in the Coulomb
   dissociation of B-8
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE solar neutrino; Coulomb dissociation; radioactive beam; E2 component;
   Pb-208(B-8,Be-7 p)Pb-208; angular distribution
ID CROSS-SECTION; LOW ENERGIES; BE-7(P,GAMMA)B-8; EXCITATION
AB Angular distributions of the Coulomb dissociation of B-8 in the field of Pb-208 at E(in) = 51.9 MeV/u were measured at 0 degrees less than or equal to theta(8) less than or equal to 10 degrees and 0.5 less than or equal to E(rel) less than or equal to 2.25 MeV. The data were analyzed using a quantum mechanical method where E1, E2 and l = 2 nuclear amplitudes are included. Although systematic effects could be large, the extracted E2 components appear to be considerably smaller than any theoretical predictions reported so far.

TI Study of the Be-7(p,gamma)B-8 reaction with the Coulomb dissociation
   method
SO JOURNAL OF THE PHYSICAL SOCIETY OF JAPAN
LA English
DT Article
DE Be-7(p,gamma)B-8; Coulomb dissociation
ID RADIATIVE-CAPTURE PROCESSES; SOLAR NEUTRINO PROBLEM; CROSS-SECTION;
   ASTROPHYSICALLY RELEVANT; NUCLEAR-REACTIONS; RADIOACTIVE BEAM; BREAKUP;
   ENERGIES; FACILITY; MODEL
AB The Coulomb-dissociation cross section for the process B-8 --> Be-7 + p in the field of Pb-208 was measured at E(B-8) = 46.5 A MeV. The Be-7(p,gamma)B-8 cross section relevant to the high-energy B-8 solar-neutrino production was extracted at E(C.M.) = 0.6 - 1.7 MeV. Two theoretical models on the structure of 8B were used to evaluate possible corrections due to M1 and E2 admixtures to the dominant E1 cross sections. Their overall effect is shown to be small regardless of the choice of the models. The present result is consistent with the results of the direct measurements of Filippone et al. and Vaughn et al. within errors. This result suggests further studies with the Coulomb-dissociation method to extract astrophysical S-17 factor at similar to 20 keV relevant to the high-energy solar-neutrino flux.

   WITH HEAVY-IONS
SO IEEE TRANSACTIONS ON NUCLEAR SCIENCE
LA English
DT Article
ID DEPENDENCE; PROTON
AB Ion-implanted silicon detectors were irradiated with 18-150 MeV O-16, 20 MeV Ar-40, and 53 MeV Xe-110. A linear increase of the leakage current was observed as a function of the particle fluence up to 2.2 x 10(8) cm(-2). Extracted damage factors are proportional to the averaged nuclear stopping power over five orders of magnitude covering heavy ions studied in the present work and also protons of 25-800 MeV energies.

TI COULOMB DISSOCIATION OF A HALO NUCLEUS BE-11 AND DIRECT BREAKUP
   MECHANISM
SO NUCLEAR PHYSICS A
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT International Symposium on Physics of Unstable Nuclei
CY OCT 31-NOV 03, 1994
CL NIIGATA, JAPAN
SP NIIGATA UNIV, FAC SCI, UNIV TOKYO, INST NUCL STUDY, INST PHYS & CHEM RES
ID NEUTRON HALO; LI-11
AB We have made a kinematically complete measurement of the Coulomb dissociation of Be-11 on Pb target at 72A MeV. The low-lying dipole strength distribution indicated the importance of the direct breakup mechanism, which was also supported by the observed effect of the Coulomb post acceleration. The E1 dominance of the reaction was confirmed by the angular distribution of Be-10 in the rest frame of Be-11.

TI COULOMB DISSOCIATION REACTION AND CORRELATIONS OF 2 HALO NEUTRONS IN
   LI-11
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID CROSS-SECTIONS; NUCLEUS LI-11; RICH NUCLEI; COLLISIONS
AB We have performed an exclusive measurement for the Coulomb dissociation reaction, Pb(Li-11,Li-9+2n)X at an incident energy of 43 A MeV. The deduced excitation energy spectrum of the Li-11 nucleus shows a prominent peak at 1 MeV with a large tail towards higher excitation energies. The relative energy spectra for the n-n and Li-9-2n sub-systems show that the excitation is dominated by the relative motion between Li-9 and the center-of-mass of the two neutrons. The above characteristics are explained by a direct Coulomb breakup mechanism with an extended 'di-neutron' model.

TI LARGE-DEFORMATION OF THE VERY NEUTRON-RICH NUCLEUS MG-32 FROM
   INTERMEDIATE-ENERGY COULOMB-EXCITATION
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
DE COULOMB EXCITATION; RADIOACTIVE BEAM; B(E2-O+-]2(+)) OF MG-32
ID GIANT-RESONANCES; RADIOACTIVE BEAM; PB-208; MEV/NUCLEON; DISSOCIATION;
   SCATTERING; SCHEMES; SN-120; NI-60; MEV/U
AB The Coulomb excitation of a very neutron-rich nucleus Mg-32 to its 2(+) State was studied using an unstable nuclear beam of Mg-32 at 49.2 MeV/u with a Pb-208 target. The B(E2) value of 454 +/- 78 e(2)fm(4) was extracted by a coupled channel analysis. The value is in good agreement with recent predictions. It confirms a large deformation for Mg-32 suggested by the low excitation energy of the 2(+) state, and points to the vanishing of the N = 20 shell gap.

TI COULOMB DISSOCIATION OF A HALO NUCLEUS BE-11 AT 72A MEV
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID INTERACTION CROSS-SECTIONS; HEAVY-ION COLLISIONS; NEUTRON-RICH NUCLEI;
   PROJECTILE FRAGMENTATION; LI-11; RADII; BEAMS
AB We have measured the excitation energy spectrum of the Be-10+n system in the Coulomb dissociation of the one-neutron-halo nucleus Be-11 on a Pb target at 72A MeV. We have determined the dipole strength distribution dB(E1)/dE(x) which shows a strong peak at about 800 keV excitation energy. The spectral shape is consistent with a direct breakup model. The Coulomb post acceleration effect has been observed also to support the direct breakup mechanism. The E1 dominance of the Coulomb dissociation is confirmed by observed angular distributions of Be-10 in the Be-11 rest frame.

TI OBSERVATION OF HE-10
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID LIGHT-NUCLEI; STATES; MODEL
AB The reactions Li-11 + CD2 --> 10He + X and Li-11 + C --> 10He + X at a beam energy of 61A MeV have been studied by measuring the triple coincidence of He-8 and two neutrons. Experimental data show a peak that can be explained as a resonance 10He, which is unbound by 1.2 +/- 0.3 MeV and its width is less than 1.2 MeV. The invariant mass spectra of He-8 + n show a peak that is consistent with the decay 10He --> He-8 + n + n.

TI EXPERIMENTAL-STUDY OF HE-8+P ELASTIC AND INELASTIC-SCATTERING
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID 3-PARTICLE DECAY; LIGHT-NUCLEI; STATES; BE-6; MODEL
AB An experimental study of He-8+p elastic scattering and a search for He-8* are performed. The excited state 8H* is observed in two independent experimental methods. The obtained parameters of the excited state are E(He-8)*=3.57+/-0.12 MeV, GAMMA=0.5+/-0.35 MeV, GAMMA(He-4+4n)/GAMMA(He-6+n+n) less-than-or-equal-to 5%.  Angular distributions for elastic and inelastic scattering are measured. The inelastic angular distribution is consistent with J(pi)=2+ for He-8(3.55)*.

TI STRONG ISOMER PRODUCTION IN FRAGMENTATION REACTIONS
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID INTRANUCLEAR CASCADE CALCULATION; MOMENTUM DISTRIBUTIONS; MODEL
   CALCULATIONS; FUSION
AB The population of the 0+ 0.228 MeV isomer of Al-26 has been measured in projectile fragmentation reactions at E/A = 65, 80, and 100 MeV. For beams of Al-27 and Si-28, the yield of the isomer was found to be approximately equal to that of the ground state, whereas for Ar-40 beams it was much weaker. The significance and utility of the surprisingly high isomer yields is discussed.

TI SEARCH FOR A BOUND-STATE OF A NEGATIVE PION AND NEUTRONS IN O-18+BE
   COLLISIONS
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW C
LA English
DT Article
ID MEV NUCLEON
AB A bound system of pi- and neutrons (pineuts) was searched for in the fragmentation region of O-18 + Be collisions at 100 A MeV. The upper limits for the production cross sections were obtained to be 0.08 and 0.20 nb at the 90% confidence level for singly charged systems pi-n2 and pi-n3, respectively.

AB From the combined analysis between interaction- and fragmentation- cross sections of He-4,He-6,He-8 incident reactions at 800 AMeV the thick neutron skins have been verified in He-6 and He-8 nuclei. SP BUNDESMINIST FORSCHUNG & TECHNOL, DEUT FORSCHUNGSGEMEINSCH, DEUT PHYS GESELL, EUROPEAN PHYS SOC, GESELL SCHWERIONENFORSCHUNG, INT UNION PURE & APPL PHYS, JOHANNES GUTENBERG UNIV MAINZ, MINIST WISSENSCH & WEITERBILDUNG RHEINLAND PFALZ, BITBURGER BRAUEREI TH SIMON GMBH, C H BOEHRINGER SOHN, COHERENT GMBH, DANFYSIK A S, EG & G ORTEC, LAMBDA PHYS, SCHOTT GLASWERKE
ID ELECTROMAGNETIC DISSOCIATION; NEUTRON HALO; DIPOLE; FRAGMENTATION;
   COULOMB; BEAMS
AB We have performed a full exclusive measurement for the Coulomb dissociation reaction, Pb(Li-11,Li-9+2n)X, at an incident energy of 43 A MeV. An excitation energy spectrum deduced from the invariant mass of the three body system, 9Li+2n, shows a prominent peak around 1 MeV excitation of Li-11 nucleus. The relative energy spectrum between the observed two neutrons shows a peak with very small energy below 100 keV, which is much smaller than the excitation energy of Li-11*. This indicates that the excitation is dominated by the relative motion between Li-9 and the center of mass of 2n system rather than that between two neutrons, which is consistent with the picture of a soft mode.

TI MEASUREMENTS OF LI-11+P AND LI-9+P ELASTIC SCATTERINGS AT 60 MEV
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID INTERACTION CROSS-SECTIONS; NUCLEAR RADII
AB Proton elastic scatterings of neutron rich nuclei Li-9 and Li-11 have been measured for the first time at E(lab)/A = 60 and 62 MeV, respectively, under the inverse kinematical conditions. While the angular distribution of Li-9 scattering follows the systematic trend from those of Li-6 and Li-7 scatterings, the Li-11 cross section is smaller by about a factor of two. Optical model calculations show that considerable changes in both real and imaginary potentials are necessary to reproduce the Li-11 data.

TI REVELATION OF THICK NEUTRON SKINS IN NUCLEI
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID INTERACTION CROSS-SECTIONS; RADII; SCATTERING
AB Thick neutron skins (approximately 0.9 fm) have been verified for the first time in He-6 and He-8 nuclei from a combined analysis of the interaction and the fragmentation cross sections of He-4, He-6, He-8 incident reactions at 800A MeV. A relativistic mean field (RMF) model was applied to He-6 and He-8 nuclei and shown to reproduce the neutron skin thicknesses very well. It is also shown that the RMF model predicts a gross linear dependence of the neutron skin thickness on the difference between the proton and the neutron Fermi energy in a wide range of nuclei. Possible observations of thick neutron skins in other nuclei, in particular in Na isotopes, are also discussed.

TI DETERMINATION OF THE DENSITY DISTRIBUTION AND THE CORRELATION OF HALO
   NEUTRONS IN LI-11
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID INTERACTION CROSS-SECTIONS; NUCLEAR RADII; LIGHT-NUCLEI; FRAGMENTATION;
   ISOTOPES; BEAMS
AB Interaction cross sections (sigma(I)) and transverse momentum P(t) distributions of Li-9 fragments in Li-11 reactions were measured using p and d targets at 800A MeV, and Be and C targets at 400.4 MeV. The density distribution of the Li-11 nucleus has been determined for the first time from these sigma(I)'s. It is confirmed that only a distribution with a long tail (halo) consistently reproduces the observed data. From a combined analysis of P(t) distributions of Li-9 and of neutrons, the momentum correlation of the two halo neutrons was extracted. It suggests that these neutrons have a strong tendency to move in the same direction.

CL SENDAI, JAPAN
SP TOHOKU UNIV, CYCLOTRON & RADIOISOTOPE CTR, GEN COMM
ID PROJECTILE
AB The Beam 44 fragment separator was built at the Bevalac of LBL for NMR studies of beta emitting nuclei. K-37, Ca-39, and Ti-43 fragments originating from Ca-40 and Ti-46 primary beams were separated by the separator for NMR studies on these nuclei. Nuclear spin polarization was created in Ca-39 and Ti-43 using the tilted foil technique (TFT), and the magnetic moment of Ti-43 was deduced. Fragment polarization was measured for K-37 and Ca-39 emitted to finite deflection angles. The Beam 44 fragment separator in combination with a proper polarization technique, such as TFT or fragment polarization, has been very effective for such NMR studies.

ID SPECTROMETER; SEPARATION; FRAGMENTS; GANIL; LISE
AB A radioactive beam facility based on projectile fragmentation, RIPS, has, been constructed at RIKEN to enable radioactive-beam experiments. The facility is characterized by the production of high-intensity beams and spin-polarized beams. Since the beginning of 1990, experiments on exotic nuclei have been extensively performed exploiting these useful features. The characteristics and the present status of the RIPS are described.

TI PROTON DECAY MEASUREMENT WITH RIPS FOR ASTROPHYSICAL INTEREST

CL SENDAI, JAPAN
SP TOHOKU UNIV, CYCLOTRON & RADIOISOTOPE CTR, GEN COMM
ID NE-19(P,GAMMA)NA-20
AB The decay property of Na-20 was studied using a Mg-20 beam to obtain a better understanding of the onset mechanism of the rapid proton process. The delayed protons were successfully measured, which correspond to one of the known 1+ states. There is no clear beta decay to the first excited 1+ state above the proton threshold in Na-20, suggesting that this state would not be the s-wave resonance as was expected before. The present result is preliminary; the final result will be published elsewhere.

TI DECAY PROPERTY OF NA-20 FOR THE ONSET MECHANISM OF THE RAPID-PROTON
   PROCESS
SO PHYSICAL REVIEW C
LA English
DT Article
ID NE-19(P,GAMMA)NA-20 REACTION; STATES; NUCLEI; MODEL; F-20
AB The decay property of Na-20 was studied using a Mg-20 beam to learn better the onset mechanism of the rapid-proton process. The delayed protons were successfully measured, which correspond to one of the possible 1+ states in Na-20. There is no clear beta decay to the first excited 1+ state above the proton threshold, suggesting that this state would not be the s-wave resonance in the thermal reaction of Ne-19 + p as was expected before. The half-life time of Mg-20 is determined to be 114+/-17 ms. The stellar reaction rate of Ne-19(p, gamma)Na-20 is also discussed based on the present experimental result.

   EARLY UNIVERSE
AB The cross section for the Li-8(He-4,n)B-11 reaction, of interest to primordial nucleosynthesis, has been measured using the radioactive beam facility of RIKEN.  The resulting reaction cross section was found to be larger than that estimated from the time reversed reaction cross section by a factor of 5.

ID BIG-BANG NUCLEOSYNTHESIS; PRIMORDIAL NUCLEOSYNTHESIS; NEUTRON DIFFUSION;
   EARLY UNIVERSE; ELEMENTS
AB The cross section for the Li-8(a, n)B-11 reaction, which is crucial to predictions of primordial nucleosynthesis in inhomogeneous models, has been measured using the radioactive-beam facility of the Institute for Physical and Chemical Research (RIKEN). The reaction cross section to all allowed B-11 states was found to be larger than that to just the B-11 ground state by about a factor of 5.

TI NEUTRON HALO IN BE-11 STUDIED VIA REACTION CROSS-SECTIONS
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID RICH NUCLEI; LIGHT-NUCLEI; RADII; LI-11
AB Reaction cross sections (sigma-R) and fragmentation cross sections (sigma-F) of reactions of a Be-11 beam on C, Al targets were measured by a transmission method at 33A MeV.  The sigma-R have been determined to be 1.56 +/- 0.03 b for Be-11 + C-12, and 2.27 +/- 0.05 b for Be-11 + Al-27.  These values are extremely large compared with the systematics of stable nuclei.  A large sigma-F has also been observed for the Be-11 --> Be-10 channel.  Model calculations using present and 790A MeV data confirm the long neutron tail (neutron halo) in the Be-11 density distribution.

TI DETERMINATION OF THE ASTROPHYSICAL N-13(P,GAMMA)O-14 CROSS-SECTION
   THROUGH THE COULOMB DISSOCIATION METHOD
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID RADIATIVE-CAPTURE PROCESSES; LI-7 BREAKUP REACTIONS; HOT CNO CYCLE;
   STELLAR ENERGIES
AB The Coulomb dissociation reaction Pb-208(O-14, N-13 p)Pb-208 was measured at E(in) = 87.5 MeV/u to determine the radiative width GAMMA-gamma of the 1- state in O-14 at E(ex) = 5.17 MeV.  This state dominates the radiative capture process N-13(p, gamma)O-14, a key reaction in the hot CNO cycle of hydrogen burning in stars.  We have deduced GAMMA-gamma = 3.1 +/- 0.6 eV with the help of a coupled channel calculation.  The validity of the technique was confirmed in the case of the Pb-208(N-13, C-12 p)Pb-208 reaction exciting the 1/2+ state in N-13 whose width is known.

TI NEGATIVE PION-PRODUCTION IN SUBTHRESHOLD HEAVY-ION COLLISIONS
SO PHYSICS LETTERS B
LA English
DT Article
ID NEUTRAL PIONS; 85A MEV; ENERGY; BEAMS; EMISSION; NE
AB Inclusive pi- spectra have been measured for N-14 + C collisions at 41A, 67A, 80A and 135A MeV, the lowest energies measured for the charged pion.  The cross sections fall exponentially with T-pi and the exponential slope factors at 90-degrees in the nucleon-nucleon center of mass frame are determined.  Energy distributions below a beam energy of 100A MeV are less steep than expected from the monotonic decrease of the slope factor down to 100A MeV.  The production mechanism of energetic pions far below threshold is discussed for several models.
